<div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of
Contents</a></font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">REPORT OF INDEPENDENT REGISTERED
PUBLIC ACCOUNTING FIRM</font></u></b><a name="ReportOfIndependentRegisteredPubl_123650"></a></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">To
Participants and Administrative Committee of</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Kroger Co. Savings Plan for Bargaining Unit Associates</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We have audited the accompanying statements of net assets available for
benefits &#151; modified cash basis of The Kroger Co. Savings Plan for Bargaining
Unit Associates as of December&nbsp;31, 2009 and 2008, and the related
statements of changes in net assets available for benefits &#151; modified cash
basis for the years then ended.&#160; These
financial statements are the responsibility of the Plan&#146;s management.&#160; Our responsibility is to express an opinion
on these financial statements based on our audits.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We conducted our audits in accordance with standards of the Public
Company Accounting Oversight Board (United States).&#160; Those standards require that we plan and
perform the audit to obtain reasonable assurance about whether the financial statements
are free of material misstatement.&#160; An
audit includes examining, on a test basis, evidence supporting the amounts and
disclosures in the financial statements.&#160;
An audit also includes assessing the accounting principles used and
significant estimates made by management, as well as evaluating the overall
financial statement presentation.&#160; We
believe that our audits provide a reasonable basis for our opinion.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As described in Note 2, these financial statements and supplemental
schedule were prepared on a modified cash basis of accounting, which is a
comprehensive basis of accounting other than accounting principles generally
accepted in the United States of America.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In our opinion, the financial statements referred to above present
fairly, in all material respects, the net assets available for benefits of the
Plan as of December&nbsp;31, 2009 and 2008, and the changes in its net assets
available for benefits for the years then ended, on the basis of accounting
described in Note 2.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our
audit was conducted for the purpose of forming an opinion on the basic
financial statements taken as a whole.&#160;
The accompanying supplemental Schedule of Assets (Held at End of Year)
is presented for the purpose of additional analysis and is not a required part
of the basic financial statements but is supplementary information required by
the Department of Labor Rules&nbsp;and Regulations for Reporting and Disclosure
under the Employee Retirement Income Security Act of 1974. The supplemental
schedule is the responsibility of the Plan&#146;s management.&#160; The supplemental schedule has been subjected
to the auditing procedures applied in our audit of the basic financial
statements and, in our opinion, is fairly stated in all material respects in
relation to the basic financial statements taken as a whole.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">/s/
Clark, Schaefer, Hackett&nbsp;&amp; Co.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Cincinnati,
Ohio</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">June&nbsp;28,
2010</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

of Contents</a></font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">THE KROGER
CO. SAVINGS PLAN FOR BARGAINING UNIT ASSOCIATES</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Notes to Financial
Statements<a name="NotesToFinancialStatements_124019"></a></font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.75pt;text-indent:-18.75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Description of Plan</font></u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.75pt;text-indent:-18.75pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following description of The Kroger Co. Savings Plan for Bargaining
Unit Associates (Plan) provides only general information.&#160; Participants should refer to the plan
document for a more complete description of Plan provisions.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">General</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Plan is sponsored by The Kroger Co., an Ohio corporation, and its wholly-owned
subsidiaries (collectively the Company).&#160;
The Plan is a defined contribution plan covering all employees of the
Company who have attained age 21, are covered by a collective bargaining agreement,
have been employed 30 days, and have completed 72 hours of service within the
30-day period. It is subject to the provisions of the Employee Retirement
Income Security Act of 1974, as amended (ERISA).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Contributions</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Subject
to certain limits, participants may contribute up to 75% of compensation per
pay period to the Plan. Participants are also permitted to deposit into the
Plan distributions from other qualified plans.&#160;
It is at the discretion of participants to modify and direct
investments. Participants are eligible to make catch-up contributions beginning
in the year in which they reach age 50.&#160;
No Company contributions are made to the Plan.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Participant Accounts</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Each
participant account is credited with the participant contribution, and an allocation
of Plan earnings or losses.&#160; Allocations
of earnings or losses are based upon the performance of the investment funds
chosen by the participant.&#160; The benefit
to which a participant is entitled is the benefit that can be provided from the
participant&#146;s vested account.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Vesting</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">All
accounts of a participant are fully vested at all times.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Benefits</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Payment
of benefits can be made under various methods, depending upon the reason for
the distribution, such as termination of service, death, or retirement, as well
as other factors.&#160; At termination, those
participants with a balance of less than or equal to $1,000 will receive a
single lump sum distribution.&#160; Absent
specific elections by the participant, those with balances greater than $1,000
and less than or equal to $5,000 shall be distributed, in the form of a direct
rollover, to an individual </font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4<a name="PB_4_123738_3641"></a></font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of Contents</a></font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">retirement
account designated by the Plan Administrator.&#160;
Those with balances greater than $5,000 may elect to leave their funds
in the Plan or choose other options.&#160;
Participants are entitled to benefits beginning at normal retirement age
(generally age 65).&#160; Benefits are
recorded when paid.&#160; Unclaimed benefits
are forfeited and are applied to pay Plan expenses.&#160; Forfeited unclaimed benefits are restored if
a participant later establishes a valid benefit claim.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Participant Loans</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Plan permits participants to borrow from their vested account. The maximum
amount that may be borrowed is the lesser of $50,000 or 50% of the vested
balance of the account.&#160; Loan terms range
from 1 - 4 years or up to 6 years for the purchase of a primary residence. The
loans are collateralized by the balance in the participant&#146;s account and bear
interest commensurate with local prevailing rates at the time the loan is made.
Principal and interest are paid through periodic payroll deductions.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Reclassifications</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Certain
prior year amounts have been reclassified to conform to the current year
presentation.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.4pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Summary of
Significant Accounting Policies</font></u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Basis of accounting</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The financial statements of
the Plan are prepared using the modified cash basis of accounting, which is the
equivalent of the accrual basis except that certain income receivable,
contributions receivable, and other accruals are not recorded. This is a
comprehensive basis of accounting other than accounting principles generally
accepted in the United States of America and is permitted under ERISA.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Master Trust</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The investments of the Plan,
along with investments of other plans of The Kroger Co. and its subsidiaries,
are located for investment purposes in a master trust pursuant to an agreement
dated July&nbsp;1, 2004 (the Master Trust), between Bank of America N.A., as
successor in interest to Merrill Lynch Bank&nbsp;&amp; Trust Co., FSB, the
trustee, and the Company.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Investment valuation and income recognition</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Plan&#146;s investments within the Master Trust are stated at fair value.&#160; Fair value is the price that would be
received to sell an asset or paid to transfer a liability in an orderly
transaction between market participants at the measurement date.&#160; See Note 6 for discussion of fair value.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Purchases
and sales of securities are recorded on a trade date basis.&#160; Gains or losses on sales of securities are
based on average cost.&#160; Interest income
and dividend income are recorded on the date received by the Plan.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5<a name="PB_5_123738_5250"></a></font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table
of Contents</a></font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Investment
contracts held by a defined contribution plan are required to be reported at
fair value. However, contract value is the relevant measurement attribute for
that portion of the net assets available for benefits of a defined-contribution
plan attributable to fully benefit-responsive investment contracts because
contract value is the amount participants would receive if they were to
initiate a permitted transaction under the terms of the Plan.&#160; The Plan invests in investment contracts
through The Kroger Defined Contribution Plan Master Trust.&#160; The Statement of Net Assets Available for
Benefits presents the fair value of the investment in the Master Trust as well
as the adjustment of the investment in the master trust from fair value to
contract value relating to investment contracts.&#160; The Statement of Changes in Net Assets
Available for Benefits is prepared on a contract value basis.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Estimates</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
presentation of financial statements in conformity with the modified cash basis
of accounting requires management to make estimates and assumptions that affect
certain reported amounts and disclosures.&#160;
Actual results may differ from those estimates.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Administrative expenses</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Plan will pay the
administrative costs and expenses of the Plan, including the trustee and
management fees.&#160; Any expenses that are
unable to be allocated to participants are paid by the Company.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Subsequent events</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company evaluates events
and transactions occurring subsequent to the date of the financial statements
for matters requiring recognition or disclosure in the financial statements.
The accompanying financial statements consider events through the date on which
the financial statements were available to be issued.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Investments</font></u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Plan provides for participant directed investments into common stock of The
Kroger Co., mutual funds, collective trusts, stable value funds, and certain
retirement date funds, through the investment in the Master Trust.&#160; Investments that represent 5% or more of the
Plan&#146;s net assets as of December&nbsp;31, 2009 and 2008 are as follows:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Included
in investment income from the Plan&#146;s investment in the Master Trust is
appreciation (depreciation) from investments bought, sold and held during the
year of $12,472,006 and $(27,132,458) for the years ended December&nbsp;31,
2009 and 2008, respectively.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6<a name="PB_6_123738_7672"></a></font></p>

<div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table
of Contents</a></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Investment Contracts</u>:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Master Trust holds several synthetic investment contracts which are
managed by investment fund managers.&#160; The
Master Trust also purchases wrapper contracts from financial institutions which
provide assurance that crediting rates will never be less than zero.&#160; All Plans have an undivided interest in each
investment contract.&#160; The investment
contracts are fully benefit-responsive.&#160;
A fully benefit-responsive investment provides a liquidity guarantee by
a financially responsible third party of principal and previously accrued
interest for liquidations, transfers, loans, or withdrawals initiated by Plan
participants under the terms of the ongoing Plan. Certain employer-initiated
events (i.e. layoffs, mergers, bankruptcy, Plan termination) are not eligible
for the liquidity guarantee.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In general, issuers may terminate the investment contracts and settle
at other than contract value if the qualification status of the employer or
plan changes, breach of material obligations under the contract and
misrepresentation by the contract holder, or failure of the underlying
portfolio to conform to the pre-established investment guidelines.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Plan Administrator does not believe that the occurrence of any such
event, which would limit the Plan&#146;s ability to transact at contract value with
participants, is probable.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following information relates to the Master Trust interest in
investment contracts (in thousands):</font></p>

value, and book value of the investment.&#160;

investments is zero.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net
investment income (loss) of the Master Trust for the year ended December&nbsp;31,
2009 and 2008 was $178,690 and $(597,682) respectively. Included in these
amounts are dividends of $59,016 and $74,594 at December&nbsp;31, 2009 and
2008, respectively.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
underlying investments within the synthetic contracts include corporate,
government and mortgage backed debt securities.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As
of December&nbsp;31, 2009 and 2008, the Plan&#146;s interest in the net assets of
the Master Trust was 2.68% and 2.06%, respectively. The Master Trust allocates
individual assets to each plan participating in the Master Trust
arrangement.&#160; Therefore, the investment
results of the Plan may not reflect its proportionate interest in the Master
Trust.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Fair Value Measurements</font></u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For
financial statement elements currently required to be measured at fair value,
Generally Accepted Accounting Principles define fair value and establish a
framework for measuring fair value and disclosing fair value measurements
utilized. The standards define fair value as the price that would be received
to sell an asset or paid to transfer a liability (exit price) regardless of
whether an observable liquid market price exists.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Generally
Accepted Accounting Principles establish a fair value hierarchy that categorizes
the inputs to valuation techniques that are used to measure fair value into
three levels:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.2in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160; Level
1 includes observable inputs which reflect quoted prices for identical assets
or liabilities in active markets at the measurement date.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8<a name="PB_8_115515_7608"></a></font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='8',FILE='C:\JMS\mweinst\10-13252-2\task4169851\13252-2-bc.htm',USER='mweinst',CD='Jun 29 09:59 2010' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table
of Contents</a></font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.2in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160; Level 2 includes observable inputs for assets or liabilities
other than quoted prices included in Level 1 and it includes valuation
techniques which use prices for similar assets and liabilities.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.2in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Level 3
includes unobservable inputs which reflect the reporting entity&#146;s estimates of
the assumptions that market participants would use in pricing the asset or
liability, including assumptions about risk.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
asset&#146;s fair value measurement level within the fair value hierarchy is based
on the lowest level of any input that is significant to the fair value
measurement. Valuation techniques used need to maximize the use of observable
inputs and minimize the use of unobservable inputs.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
following is a description of the valuation methods used for assets measured at
fair value. There have been no changes in methodologies used at
December&nbsp;31, 2009 and 2008.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.2in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Cash
and cash equivalents: </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The carrying value approximates fair value.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.2in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Common
Stocks: </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The fair values of these securities are based on observable market
quotations for identical assets and are valued at the closing price reported on
the active market on which the individual securities are traded.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.2in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Mutual Funds:</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> The fair
values of these securities are primarily based on observable market quotations
for identical assets and are valued at the closing price reported on the active
market on which the individual securities are traded.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.2in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Guaranteed Investment
Contracts: The investments include cash and cash equivalents, fixed maturity
guaranteed investment contracts (GICs) and constant duration GICs. The fair
value of the investments are calculated using the present value of the
contracts future cash flow values discounted by comparable duration Wall Street
Journal GIC Index rates. Fair values for variable synthetic GICs are calculated
using the present value of the contract&#146;s future cash flow values discounted by
comparable swap rates. Fair values for constant duration synthetic GICs are
calculated using the market values provided by the external investment
managers. </font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.2in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Collective Trusts: The
collective trust funds are public investment vehicles valued using a Net Asset
Value (NAV) provided by the manager of each fund.&#160; The NAV is based on the underlying net assets
owned by the fund, divided by the number of shares outstanding.&#160; The NAV&#146;s unit price is quoted on a private
market that is not active.&#160; However, t</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">he NAV is based
on the fair value of the underlying securities within the fund, which are
traded on an active market, and valued at the closing price reported on the
active market on which those individual securities are traded.&#160; The significant investment strategies of the
funds are as described in the financial statements provided by each fund.&#160; There are no restrictions on redemptions from
these funds.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.2in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Retirement Date Funds:</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> Retirement date funds are
made up of investments in mutual funds, custom funds, and collective trusts,
and are valued in a manner consistent with that described above for Mutual
Funds and the Interest in Master Trust. </font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9<a name="PB_9_120041_8146"></a></font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of
Contents</a></font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .55in;text-indent:-.2in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Participant Loans:</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> Participant loans are valued at their
outstanding amortized balances, which approximate fair value.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
methods described above may produce a fair value calculation that may not be
indicative of net realizable value or reflective of future fair values.
Furthermore, while the Plan believes its valuations methods are appropriate and
consistent with other market participants, the use of different methodologies
or assumptions to determine the fair value of certain financial instruments
could result in a different fair value measurement.&#160; Investment securities, in general, are
exposed to various risks, such as interest rate, credit and overall market
volatility.&#160; Due to the level of risk
associated with certain investment securities, it is reasonably possible that
changes in the fair values of investment securities will occur in the near term
and, that such changes could materially affect the amounts reported in the
statements of net assets available for benefits.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">While
all the investments of the participating plans are deemed part of the Master
Trust, each plan does maintain a separate accounting of its share of the
investments in the Master Trust, which is reflected below.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
following table sets forth by level, within the fair value hierarchy, the Plan&#146;s
assets at fair value as of December&nbsp;31, 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

GICs shown above include wrap contracts, the fair value of which is immaterial.</font></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;"><a href="#TableOfContents" title="Click to go to Table of Contents">Table of

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Income Tax Status</u>:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Plan obtained its latest
determination letter on December&nbsp;3, 2004, in which the Internal Revenue
Service stated that the Plan, as then designed, complied with the applicable
requirements of the Internal Revenue Code (IRC). The Plan has been amended
since receiving this letter. However, the Plan administrator believes that the
Plan is designed and is currently being operated in compliance with the
applicable requirements of the IRC. Therefore, no provision for income taxes
has been included in the Plan&#146;s financial statements.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Plan
Termination</font></u><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Although it has not expressed any intent to do so, the Company has the
right under the Plan to terminate the Plan at any time subject to the
provisions of ERISA.&#160; In the event of any
total or partial termination or discontinuance, the accounts of all affected
participants shall remain fully vested and non-forfeitable.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9.&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; <u>Related-party and
Party-in-interest Transactions</u></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:.3pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Plan&#146;s portion of its interest in the Master Trust included $5,027,772 and
$5,666,296 of The Kroger Co. common shares at December&nbsp;31, 2009 and 2008,
respectively, at fair value.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:.3pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Plan purchased 161,825 and 228,927 shares of The Kroger Co. common shares at a
cost of $3,524,245 and $6,082,290 in 2009 and 2008, respectively through its
interest in the Master Trust.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:.3pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Plan sold 129,479 and 200,504 shares of The Kroger Co. common shares for
$2,799,613 and $5,369,453 with a realized loss of $(66,728) in 2009 and a
realized gain of $203,141 in 2008, through its interest in the Master Trust.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:.3pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Bank
of America, N.A. and Merrill Lynch provide recordkeeping and investment
management services to the Plan.&#160;
Therefore, transactions with Bank of America, N.A. and Merrill Lynch
qualify as party-in-interest transactions.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10.&#160; <u>Reconciliation of Financial Statements to Form&nbsp;5500</u>:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-18.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:.3pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
following is a reconciliation of net assets available for benefits per the
financial statements to the Form&nbsp;5500:</font></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit&nbsp;23.1</font></b></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">CONSENT OF
INDEPENDENT REGISTERED PUBLIC ACCOUNTING FIRM</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">To
the Plan Administrator of</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Kroger Co. Savings Plan For Bargaining Unit Associates:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We
consent to incorporation by reference in the Registration Statements (No.&nbsp;333-164951
and 333-152606) on Form&nbsp;S-8 of The Kroger Co. of our report dated June&nbsp;28,
2010, relating to the statements of net assets available for benefits of The
Kroger Co. Savings Plan For Bargaining Unit Associates as of December&nbsp;31, 2009 and 2008, and
the related statements of changes in net assets available for benefits and the
supplemental schedule for the years then ended, which report appears in the December&nbsp;31, 2009 annual report
on Form&nbsp;11-K of The Kroger Co. Savings Plan For Bargaining Unit
Associates.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">/s/
Clark, Schaefer, Hackett&nbsp;&amp; Co.</font></p>
